{"nick":"joepie91","message":"for example: \"let's use a composite UNIQUE constraint to make sure every relation between two things is unique\"","date":"2017-07-21T09:27:10.062Z","type":"message"}

{"nick":"joepie91","message":"whereas with a regular relation, you always have one column for the one type, and one column for the other type, and the order is known upfront","date":"2017-07-21T09:28:05.815Z","type":"message"}
